#### test

* environment
  * Revision 795
  * MINGW64
  * chrome
* httpserver2
  * -v   : verbose (console log)
  * -d   : debug libhotplace-sdk inside
  * -k   : keylog
  * -D 2 : trace level to debug
  * -T   : use trial instead of libssl

````
$ ./test-httpserver2.exe -v -d -r -D 2 -T -k &
````
